Check the package content at the beginning of the on-site check-in, and learn each item at the same time as the guests check-in. It's really embarrassing. The dinner included in the package is actually in another Songpin Hotel. It takes ten minutes to take a shuttle bus to another hotel for dinner. It is also called an upgrade. In fact, the Yue restaurant in the hotel is closed, and the hotel swimming pool is not available. It is also said that it is under maintenance. , Welcome fruit, don't ask, don't send it at all. It is said that no one avoids wasting the room by calling. Is it lonely for me to redeem the rights? Even if there are more than two bottles of mineral water in the room, it costs ten yuan a bottle. There are countless people who stay in five-star hotels and have never heard that basic drinking water is not enough... The most annoying thing is that breakfast is like checking the number of thieves It was to check the package and to implement the main station. Fortunately, I pulled out an entry on the mobile phone booking interface, showing two big and one small... I always misunderstood that such a strict inspection would require hundreds of dishes, seafood, and Bordeaux. Let's go, only to find out that there are not enough seasonings to add 20 kinds, the waiter's attitude is cold and there is no smile, the air conditioner in the room is getting hotter and hotter in the 1980s As soon as you take it, the power will be cut off immediately. The so-called suite is just two connected rooms. Therefore, we advise guests who have principles of room and service to choose carefully. When I checked out, I reported the problem to the front desk. The lobby manager apologized and was very sincere, but one person cannot support a hotel. What is needed is the system and norms, and the team should not add to the chaos. Finally, I am very grateful to the lobby manager for sending the car to the parking lot and then to Sea World. By the way, both Sea World and Snow World are very worth playing. You can queue up at different peaks when you play Sea World first on the second floor. Novices in Snow World must find a coach for a better experience.
